#include "testutils.h"

#include "sha3.h"

const struct nettle_hash nettle_shake256 =
  {
   "shake256",
   sizeof(struct sha3_256_ctx),
   0,
   SHA3_256_BLOCK_SIZE,
   (nettle_hash_init_func *) sha3_256_init,
   (nettle_hash_update_func *) sha3_256_update,
   (nettle_hash_digest_func *) sha3_256_shake,
  };
